 The Shitala Saptami or Ashtami fast is observed on the Saptami and Ashtami dates of the Krishna Paksha of Chaitra month
 is saal yah vrath 27 or 28 march ko rakhaa ja rahaa he
 On this day, people keep Sheetla Mata fast and worship them
 puja karne ke baad bhakt maa sheetala ko thanda basi prasad kaa bhoga lagaate hai
 Let us know why their devotees offer bati prasad to Mata Sheetla
 hindu dharm ke anusaar har upwas ko kholte samay bhagwaan ko shuddh taaja bane prasad kaa bhoga lagane kaa niyam he
 But this rule does not apply in the fast of Mata Sheetla
 is din log apane gharon main taaja bhojan nahin banaate hai
 It is custom to eat cold food on this day
 dharmik karansheetla ashtami ke din basi prasad kaa bhoga lagane ke peeche kaha jaataa he ki mata sheetala ko thanda bhojan ati priy he
 According to religious beliefs, the name of Mata Sheetla means cold
 yahi vajah he ki log sheetala devi ko prasann karne ke liye unhen thandi chizon kaa bhoga lagaate hai
 In North India, Sheetla Saptami or Ashtami fast is also known as Basoda
 aisa isliye bhi he kyonki is din ke baad log basi bhojan grahan karnaa band kar dete hai
 It is believed that this day is the last day of this season when a person can eat stale food
 mana jaataa he ki sheetala devi kaa vrath karne se sheetala devi prasann hoti hai
 Due to which, all the diseases of the eyes and the defects caused by Sheetla are removed
 sheetala mata bacchon kii sehat kii raksha karti hai
 At the same time, wealth fills wealth
 sheetala mata devi kii tarah hoti hai, jo gardabh yani gadhe par savaar hoti hai
 He has a broom in his hand
 neem ke patton ko jevar kii tarah pahane hoti hai
 There is also a urn of cold water in one of his hands
 mata saafe safai, swasthy jivan or sheetaltaa kii pratik hai

 - is din gangaajal daalkar snaan karen
 Wear orange clothes
 - dopaher 12 baje sheetala mandir jaakar mata kii puja karen
 Worship the mother by putting fragrant flowers, neem leaves and fragrant perfumes
 - sheetala mata ko thande yaa basi khaane kaa bhoga lagaaein
 - Perform aarti by burning camphor
 - sheetala matrai namah mantra kaa jaap karen
 Importance of stale food - Cold and stale food is eaten at home on Sheetla Ashtami
 is din subah ke samay ghar main chulhaa nahin jalaate hai

 - is din thanda basi pua, puri, daal bhaat, mithai kaa mata ko bhoga lagaakar khaaya jaataa he
 - You should also donate food before eating

 ) centre sarkaar cashles tranjection ko badhaava dene ke liye jor-shor se juty he
 The central government has ordered all its ministries and offices to adopt e-pension
 vitt mantralay kii ore se jari aadesh ke mutabik 5000 se zyada len-dein main i-pement ko apanaaya jaae
 The ministry has ordered this order to be implemented immediately to all ministries and offices attached to it

 Makar Sankranti 2019: makar sankranti tyohaar kaa khaas mahatv hota he
 It is a festival of happiness
 alag-alag shaharon main is parv ko alag-alag naam se manaaya jaataa he
 It is believed that at the time of Makar Sankranti, the sun is Uttarayan
 is samay kiye gaye daan kaa fal baaki dinon ke mukaable kai guna zyada hota he
 It is believed that at the time of Makar Sankranti, the sun meets its son i
e
 Shani
 shukr kaa udai bhi makar sankranti par hi hota he
 That is why all auspicious works begin with this festival
 is din daan, puja, jaap snaan aadi chizon kaa bahut mahatv hota he
 But there are some things which are considered forbidden to do on Makar Sankranti
 makar sankranti par bhuulakar bhi na karen ye 5 kaam-1
